	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	$tmp = pathinfo('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('dev/generate_wellknown_other_sqlite', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

}

	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql');
	$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_12();
if (!is_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql');
} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql') != '3475c381264f1e0df2fdddf1d6c433cfb0801524') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/wellknown_other_sqlite.sql');
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_17();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') != '2cdbc4c8648b4eccad8167bd2def7ca8f70dd69b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '2cdbc4c8648b4eccad8167bd2def7ca8f70dd69b') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '06e85b4bd7224fba7a86294b43067db0c8b36237') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_17();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio') !== '2cdbc4c8648b4eccad8167bd2def7ca8f70dd69b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	writefile_18();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') != '03170e23c7682f6f52b5d7c8b45a37abb571055c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/class_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '03170e23c7682f6f52b5d7c8b45a37abb571055c') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== 'c0070c1f315e47f9d643ea73cb517b7181e5ca44') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/classes/class_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/class_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_18();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/class_diagram.png') !== '03170e23c7682f6f52b5d7c8b45a37abb571055c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/class_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/config_values.txt');
	writefile_19();
	if (!is_file('includes/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/config_values.txt') != '098628bcf0c6b6aa3e4a1525ea3ac8082aba7438') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/config_values.txt') !== '098628bcf0c6b6aa3e4a1525ea3ac8082aba7438') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/config_values.txt') !== '7e626e993ccd74c91ee854c7aad7cf15e391cae5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_19();

if (!is_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	writefile_20();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') != 'c5b239ca68e9c0f2f5199a8230c6abe45c876d0b') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== 'c5b239ca68e9c0f2f5199a8230c6abe45c876d0b') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== 'd50b45b8f086ab73cbe789c40ec6e2ad85604b38') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_20();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio') !== 'c5b239ca68e9c0f2f5199a8230c6abe45c876d0b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.drawio');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') != 'e5951124e7a84fee421bfc3a61e72e7677187901') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== 'e5951124e7a84fee421bfc3a61e72e7677187901') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== '7999f70b24fe6859fbc6fe83babb2b399e6f801d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png') !== 'e5951124e7a84fee421bfc3a61e72e7677187901') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/database_connectivity_diagram.png');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_22();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') != '77d246473af54ae29dc6682f4cd9e2de1a2a3c2e') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '77d246473af54ae29dc6682f4cd9e2de1a2a3c2e') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '59bcd9402b5012990daa80abf53ad2533697384e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_22();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php') !== '77d246473af54ae29dc6682f4cd9e2de1a2a3c2e') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/mysqli/plugin.inc.php');
		}
	}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') != 'cf4b511ffb8a5329fb9985405de6c28c2157a6f8') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {

	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') !== 'cf4b511ffb8a5329fb9985405de6c28c2157a6f8') {

			if (!@copy('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php') !== 'cf4b511ffb8a5329fb9985405de6c28c2157a6f8') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/odbc/plugin.inc.php');

	writefile_24();
	if (!is_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') != '55dc346096344221cda9e2b13a8707d7737672b0') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== '55dc346096344221cda9e2b13a8707d7737672b0') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== 'c8e4cc0fe37883450bdfe6186ecea653a12da736') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_24();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php') !== '55dc346096344221cda9e2b13a8707d7737672b0') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/database/pdo/plugin.inc.php');

	}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');
	writefile_27();
	if (!is_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php') != '2aad53e00af959175e1c3cb3c66c7d8a085b3d0c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php') !== '2aad53e00af959175e1c3cb3c66c7d8a085b3d0c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php') !== '9383fc07b887c013e53920ebb8896ad16959ecce') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php') !== '2aad53e00af959175e1c3cb3c66c7d8a085b3d0c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/publicPages/090_login/plugin.inc.php');
		}
